## Diagram 3

```mermaid
graph LR
    A[.Values.rbac.install] -->|condition| B[ServiceAccount Resource]
    B --> C[metadata.name]
    B --> D[metadata.namespace]
    B --> E[metadata.labels]
    F[.Release.Namespace] --> D
    G[sscd.labels template] --> E
```

    SetMetadata --> ApplyLabels
    ApplyLabels --> [*]
    Skip --> [*]
